import javax.persistence.Entity;
import javax.persistence.Id;

@Entity
public class Dummy {
  
  @Id
  private Long id;

  public Long getId() {
    return id;
  }

  public void setId(Long id) {
    this.id = id;
  }

}

------------------

import javax.persistence.Entity;

@Entity
public class DummyA extends Dummy {

  private String name;

  public String getName() {
    return name;
  }

  public void setName(String name) {
    this.name = name;
  }
  
}

------------------

import javax.persistence.Entity;

@Entity
public class DummyB extends Dummy {

  private DummyEmbedded embedded;

  public DummyEmbedded getEmbedded() {
    return embedded;
  }

  public void setEmbedded(DummyEmbedded embedded) {
    this.embedded = embedded;
  }

}

------------------

import javax.persistence.Embeddable;

@Embeddable
public class DummyEmbedded {

  private int x;

  public int getX() {
    return x;
  }

  public void setX(int x) {
    this.x = x;
  }
}


------------------

public class DummyTest extends BaseTest {

  public void testDummy() throws Exception {
    EntityManager em = EntityManagerSingleton.get();
    EntityTransaction tx = em.getTransaction();
    tx.begin();
    
    DummyA d = new DummyA(); 
    d.setId(new Long(1000));
    
    em.persist(d);
    tx.commit();
    em.close();
  }
}
